<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Transfer Learning</h2><a id="user-content-transfer-learning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Transfer Learning" href="#transfer-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Train on <a href="http://www.liangzheng.com.cn/Project/project_reid.html" rel="nofollow">Market-1501</a>, Test on DukeMTMC-reID</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The primary motivation is that collecting ID annotation is relatively-expensive in human resource and time cost.</p>
<p dir="auto">Is it possible to use less annotation on the unseen dataset, especially ID labels?</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Methods</th>
<th>Use DukeMTMC Training Data (without ID label but may use the camera ID)</th>
<th>Rank@1</th>
<th>mAP</th>
<th>Reference</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>UMDL</td>
<td>✔️</td>
<td>18.5%</td>
